    (function () {

        var handler;
        var errorHandler;
        var error;
        var response;
        var timeout;

        
        if (!window.hasOwnProperty('numCraftFastPrefetches')) {
            window.numCraftFastPrefetches = 0;
        }
        window.numCraftFastPrefetches++;
        
        function registerHandler(onSuccess, onError) {
            if (handler) throw new Error('handler already registered');
            handler = onSuccess;
            errorHandler = onError || function () {};
            if (true) {
                timeout = setTimeout(maybeCallHandler);
            } else {
                maybeCallHandler();
            }
        }
        
        function maybeCallHandler() {
            clearTimeout(timeout);
            delete timeout;
            if (error !== undefined && errorHandler) {
                errorHandler(error);
            } else if (response && handler) {
                handler(response);
            }
        }
        registerHandler.responseReceived = function(receivedResponse) {
            response = receivedResponse;
            window.numCraftFastPrefetches--;
            if (window.numCraftFastPrefetches === 0) {
                if (window.performance && window.performance.now) {
                    window.timingCraftPrefetchDone = Math.round(window.performance.now());
                }
                if (!!console.timeStamp) {
                    console.timeStamp('craft_fast_prefetch_done');
                }
                // Never mark craft fast prefetches again
                window.numCraftFastPrefetches = Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER;
            }
            maybeCallHandler();
        }
        registerHandler.responseError = function(receivedError) {
            error = receivedError
            maybeCallHandler()
        }
        
        registerHandler.getDataIfAvailable = function() {
            if (response) {
                return { payload: response };
            }
            if (error) {
                return { error: error };
            }
            return undefined;
        }
